< Text>
I HIGHLY recommend this store. Catilla Smith was our sales rep and I can't say enough good things about her. She was extremely knowledgeable about every mattress and we really felt as if she took the time to get to know each of our bodies so that she could recommend the right mattresses for us in our price range. We were not easy customers and she was extremely patient with us and honestly cared that we took our time and found the perfect mattress.

This was the 1st of 3 mattress stores my boyfriend and I went to look at mattresses. We hadn't done much research on pricing and had a gift card to a department store so we wanted to shop around a bit. The department store staff was terrible and compared to Catilla and their prices were too high even with our $200 gift card! We then went to a similar mattress store to Mattress Discounters. The staff in the other store didn't even compare to Catilla! We got a quote on one of the mattresses and it was a bit higher than Mattress Depot. We knew we could get them to beat Mattress Depot's price, but we were so happy with Catilla's customer service that we wanted to return and give her the business.

In the end we couldn't be happier with our purchase and the service we received from the entire Mattress Depot staff, but especially Catilla!!! We will definitely return for future business!</Text>

< Text>
DON'T WALK, RUN AWAY FROM THIS PLACE

(Lived here for over 20 years & was transferred into a remodeled apartment)

The new management here is cruel, unkind and hardhearted. The have incited a venomous hatred in the tenets that I have never seen before. The tenants are treated like a nuisance when they're not being completely ignored.
This is a very abridged version of my experience.
I had started the process of getting an apartment here in April, my credit and background check came back and it was all good.
Around May I had been told that I had an apartment only to have them tell me they had given it to someone else.
About a month or so later I was brought in to sign my lease at which point they told me my deposit had not been paid (I thought it had, I was never told otherwise) and that I had 30 minutes to give them almost 1000 dollars as a deposit or I'd loose my apartment. The thing is loosing that apartment meant I would likely loose my section 8. They had 3 months to make me aware of the deposit. Based on their previous actions toward me and other tenets here I would have to say this was done on purpose. By the end of the 3 months of dealing with this management I felt mentally and emotionally battered.

The several people that I know who moved here including myself where moved into dirty and apparently unsafe apartments, as this place has asbestos in the walls and the apartments have large holes, cracks and gaps in the walls often hidden by cabinets.
Elderly, pregnant and disabled persons were moved in duriing a heat wave and did not have working AC and were ignored by the management when they asked for help. And this is normal for this place. It's so bad a petition was started to get one of the managers removed. Several people had to get lawyers to get the management  to meet basic needs. Not even if section8 says they HAVE to fix something do they fix it. They treat the people here like cattle. It's sickening.
This is supposed to be a non smoking complex. But it's not. There is and abnormally high number of smokers living here. I literally have never seen so many smokers in one place in all my life. Management will do NOTHING when you tell them your neighbors are filling your apartment with pot smoke. My apartment permanently smells like a skunk got run over during a forest fire. They don't care if you have asthma and they really don't care if it's making you ill.
If you have pretty much any complaint at all nothing will be done about it if you don't get a lawyer. Also bizarrely,  I was told by management that to make a complaint you have to email them. They refuse to except complaints in person or over the phone. I have emailed them multiple times about problems. I have never gotten a response back. I 100% know I have the wright email.
I know a woman who lives here, her neighbor smokes pot filling her apartment with smoke and plays music so loud it vibrates her walls and bed. She hasn't been able to sleep in her apartment since he moved in next to her. She complained... guess what management ignored her.
People here are not normal or right in the head including management. For example in July or August there was and arson by some of the people who live here. It's not a safe place.
The renovations have been poorly done. A few examples being, in the beginning some the the windows were put in backwards. I'm constantly getting electrical shocks from the switches and I'm not the only one. When the tubs were repainted large chunks of visible grit became stuck to the fresh paint. It looks bad but feels worse on your feet.
Nails, screws, and razor blades where left inside and on the grounds of the apartments.
The one bedroom unites are advertised as having walking closets but only a portion of them have this.
Some of the apartments have significant mold and water damage from leaking roofs and pipes, none of which was fixed in the renovations. They just paint over the mold and caulk over the leaks.

If you value you sanity, health and safety don't move here.< /Text>

<username>Jared Cohee</username><date>1578934562929<//date>< rating>
5< /rating>
<review>VIETNAM
Excerpt from Eat the World Los Angeles:
If you have ever spent time in Vietnam, one of many vivid memories is the smell of fresh breads early in the morning. Banh mi vendors set up their carts before the sun comes up, stacking loaves of French-style baguettes in front of their work stations, ready to be carved up and stuffed with meats, pickled vegetables, condiments, and spicy peppers.

The early morning nature of this sandwich should be taken into account when searching for the right banh mi shop. To be honest, any place that waits to open for lunch and promises a good sandwich is probably lying. The Beach Blvd shopping plaza that Lynda Sandwich lives in actually has two early opening banh mi places, but skip the chain behemoth and stop in here for your sandwich and coffee.

The dac biet Lynda special will set you back the princely sum of $4.25, an incredible deal just like most in Orange County. "Dac biet" is seen on menus across the Vietnamese food spectrum and basically translates as they have here: Daily special. Here at Lynda that means a layer of pork pâté, thin slices of Vietnamese pork roll, and grilled chicken. These meats are joined by a mayo full of garlic and a lot of white pepper hiding somewhere. Pickled carrots and daikon bring crunch and sweetness, while fresh cucumber and cilantro add a cooling element.<//review>< Pics>

Vinh Ha< /Name>
<Date>1577589426953< /Date><rate>4<//rate>< Text>
After all these years, I finally decided to give this spot a try. There was ample parking even though inside had many people. It had a lively atmosphere with music and people were actually hanging out or dining in! That's a real surprise for me since I did not expect that from a banh mi place LOL.

Some reviews I read said their sandwiches had too much bread. I don't see how that's possible seeing how they use a very thin bread that's crispy. I ordered the Dac Biet (Special) and one of the Trung Lap Xuong (egg/sausage). The Dac Biet to me was just "okay." The bread was cold but still crispy. There was not a whole lot inside the bread and it did feel like it was a bit lacking. The only thing that saves it is the mayo that they use it. Such a good flavor! I'd still rather get a Dac Biet elsewhere though. The Trung Lap Xuong sandwich however, since it has egg in it, I could tell was freshly made. The bread crispy and warm... and inside was oozing with flavor. WOW! This is my new go-to for this type of sandwich.

The customer service here was much better than a typical banh mi place as well. They call your togo order by name. They bring your order to your table and serve it as if you were in a restaurant. I will definitely come back! This is definitely a unique banh mi place compared to all the others that pop up nowadays.< /Text>

<username>Deborah Weinstein</username>< Review>
Lynda Sandwich was mentioned in Orange Coast magazine, so we went out of our way to find it when an errand took us to Westminster. It’s a bright and inviting space.  Much thought and imagination has gone into decor and seating.  The rest room is gorgeous, not what you’d expect in a sandwich place.  There is techno-pop music over the loudspeaker system which is not to my taste but would have been OK without the feedback problem that turned it into a noisy racket several times during our short meal.  We ordered fish cake sandwiches at around $5 each. They came quickly and were fresh and tasty.  Over all, If a side of any kind had been included I would have scored this place five stars rather than four.  Quick and inexpensive, maybe a little skimpy.</Review>

<rate>4< /rate><Text>I've been eyeing this place every since I started looking for beignets close to home, but I'm soooo lazy that I never wanted to drive here.  Well my dealership is a block away and while I was chilling in the waiting area I pulled up my good old Yelp app and saw that this place was .2 miles away.  I jumped up and started walking over.  I really just wanted to have some beignets but I was so hungry because I didn't eat anything so far I also ordered a bbq pork banh mi and a order of the classic power sugar beignets.  The banh mi was really good, it kind of surprised me.  They didn't put mayonnaise in it (I'm anti-mayonnaise), but I believe I saw butter and bits of garlic that made me fall in love.  I thought I was ordering 1 beignet that would be donut size but it was a huge order of smaller triangle sized ones.  Fresh out of the fryer they are made to order and came out hot and oh so delicious.  Way too many for me to eat and I was starved, but I managed to eat about half.  When I left I had to take the leftovers home and the guy at the counter said that he was actually impressed by how many I ate(not sure if that was a fat joke).  Great service and it looks like they remodeled the place, it's hip/trendy paint job decor.

Way too many beignets.  I don't know if I should complain about this but I would love to see a smaller portion at a lower price.

Scratch another place off my long list of bookmarks.  This will be my go to place when ever I take my car to get service.  Solid food and service.  Don't tell anybody but the female clientele and employees are pretty cute.  Totally worth grabbing some tea/coffee and people watch.</Text>< user>

<review>Compared to banh mi che cali and lee sandwich, their quality is 8/10. I order various sandwiches here about twice a month. Each time the spread of meat/mayo/veggies is even and filling throughout both sides of the loaf, bread is still crispy even at the end of the day, and they don't skip the paté with soy sauce.

Bún bò is light in lemongrass, very very oily from the red annato flavoring and you dont feel any salt aftertaste. Lots and lots of tender beef in thin round noodle which is a plus! Cilantro, mint and viet basil were already piled on top in two inch stems (I tore off the leaves since its more appetizing to eat). The small cafe sua da is better elsewhere for $2.95. Overall great quality of ingredients, moderate flavors and priced accordingly at $8.25. Will have to come back for the sea salt vn coffee.<//review><Pictures>None</Pictures><Response>None<//Response>< Gmap_id>
